[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA double-free error was detected in libxml2’s XML parser during fuzz testing. [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reports that the function `xmlParseAttribute2` frees the same [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory region twice when handling certain malformed inputs. The issue manifests as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man AddressSanitizer abort triggered by the fuzzing harness in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Description  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running the libxml2 fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, AddressSanitizer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreports an attempt to free the same pointer twice inside `xmlParseAttribute2`. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash stack shows two distinct calls to `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the same [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m-byte allocation, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to an abort with SCARINESS [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a memory corruption vulnerability of the double-free category.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations and Findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The first free occurs in `xmlParseAttribute2` at parser.[0m[1;92mc:9024[0m[39m, and the second [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree at parser.[0m[1;92mc:9028[0m[39m.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Both frees happen on a buffer allocated earlier by `xmlFuzzMalloc` → [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlStrndup` → `xmlParseAttribute2`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` invokes `xmlCtxtParseDocument`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich in turn calls `xmlParseDocument`, `xmlParseElement`, and ultimately [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseAttribute2`.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness code merely provides input to the parser; it is not responsible for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe double-free itself.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas to Investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand the full impact and root of this double-free, review the following [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode sections:  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. parser.c:  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - xmlParseStartTag2 [0m[1;39m([0m[39minvocation chain[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
